m\n}\n\ntype LeveledCompactorOptions struct {\n\t// PE specifies the postings encoder. It is called when compactor is writing out the postings for a label name/value pair during compaction.\n\t// If it is nil then the default encoder is used. At the moment that is the \"raw\" encoder. See index.EncodePostingsRaw for more.\n\tPE index.PostingsEncoder\n\t// MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize is the max block chunk segment size. If it is 0 then the default chunks.DefaultChunkSegmentSize is used.\n\tMaxBlockChunkSegmentSize int64\n\t// MergeFunc is used for merging series together in vertical compaction. By default storage.NewCompactingChunkSeriesMerger(storage.ChainedSeriesMerge) is used.\n\tMergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc\n\t// EnableOverlappingCompaction enables compaction of overlapping blocks. In Prometheus it is always enabled.\n\t// It is useful for downstream projects like Mimir, Cortex, Thanos where they have a separate component that does compaction.\n\tEnableOverlappingCompaction bool\n}\n\nfunc NewLeveledCompactorWithChunkSize(ctx context.Context, r prometheus.Registerer, l log.Logger, ranges []int64, pool chunkenc.Pool, maxBlockChunkSegmentSize int64, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc) (*LeveledCompactor, error) {\n\treturn NewLeveledCompactorWithOptions(ctx, r, l, ranges, pool, LeveledCompactorOptions{\n\t\tMaxBlockChunkSegmentSize: prometheus.Registerer, l log.Logger, ranges []int64, pool chunkenc.Pool, opts LeveledCompactorOptions) (*LeveledCompactor, error) {\n\tif len(ranges) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"at least one opts.EnableOverlappingCompaction,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\ntype dirMeta struct {\n\tdir  string\n\tmeta *BlockMeta\n}\n\n// Plan returns a list of compactable blocks in the provided directory.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar dms []dirMeta\n\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n\t}\n\treturn c.plan(dms)\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn -1\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn 1\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn 0\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n\n\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n\t}\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\n// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n\n\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\tOuter:\n\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn p\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn overlappingDirs\n}\n\n// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n//\n// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\nfunc splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n\t\t\tt0    int64\n\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n\t\t)\n\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn splitDirs\n}\n\n// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n// and adjusting compaction level. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_018wSxTjXvpFaas4V6NuuziT","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01XTNEtwX7Bwm5rMJziUeqxC","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What Compaction Does\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction is a crucial maintenance process that merges overlapping time blocks, removes tombstoned series, and maintains query performance over time. The compaction process:\n\n- **Merges overlapping blocks**: Combines blocks with overlapping time ranges into a single, deduplicated block\n- **Removes deleted series**: Reclaims disk space by eliminating tombstoned (deleted) series data\n- **Reorganizes data**: Creates larger, better-structured blocks for improved query efficiency\n- **Manages WAL**: Converts in-memory Write-Ahead Log (WAL) data into persisted blocks\n\n### Why Compaction Is Needed\n\nWithout compaction, Prometheus would:\n- Accumulate many small blocks, slowing down queries\n- Retain deleted data indefinitely, wasting disk space\n- Have fragmented data with overlapping time ranges causing inefficient query execution\n- Build up an excessively large WAL\n\n### Compaction Levels and Block Structure\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction** strategy with exponential block ranges:\n\n- **Level 0 blocks**: Raw blocks created directly from WAL data (2 hours by default, `MinBlockDuration`)\n- **Level 1+ blocks**: Result of compacting multiple Level 0 blocks\n- **Block ranges**: By default: 2h, 6h, 18h, 54h, 162h, etc. (exponential with step size 3)\n\nEach block is identified by:\n- **ULID**: Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier with timestamp\n- **MinTime/MaxTime**: Time range of data in milliseconds\n- **Compaction.Level**: Current compaction level\n- **Compaction.Parents**: References to source blocks\n\n### When Compaction Is Triggered\n\n#### Time-Based (Automatic)\n\nCompaction triggers when the head block reaches `MinBlockDuration` (2 hours):\n\n1. **Head block compaction**: When `head.compactable()` returns true\n   - Head contains data older than MinBlockDuration/2\n   - Triggered in the main compaction goroutine loop\n   - Result: New persistent block created, WAL truncated\n\n2. **Block merging**: Triggered by the compaction plan\n   - Blocks are selected for merging based on size and level\n   - Selection follows `LeveledCompactor.selectDirs()` logic\n   - Algorithm ensures blocks are merged level-by-level\n\n#### Size-Based (Opportunistic)\n\nThe compaction planner also triggers compaction for:\n- **Tombstone cleanup**: Blocks with >5% deleted series (tombstones) are recompacted\n- **Overlapping blocks**: Vertical compaction for blocks with overlapping time ranges\n- **Failed blocks**: Blocks marked with `Compaction.Failed` are skipped in subsequent plans\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\nMonitor these metrics to track compaction health:\n\n#### Compaction Execution\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | N/A (baseline) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total triggered compactions | Rapid increase indicates issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions | > 0 (indicates failures) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Compaction execution time | P95 > 5min suggests slowdown |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to disabled auto-compact | Increases if manual intervention |\n\n#### Block Management\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded persistent blocks | > 100 (too many blocks) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total block storage size in bytes | Approaches max or disk limit |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max block retention bytes | Should match config |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases with out-of-order data |\n\n#### Compaction Progress\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Currently writing block (1 = in progress) | Should return to 0 |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact for tombstone removal | P95 > 30s suggests large blocks |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Behavior\n\n**Healthy indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increases regularly (every 2-5 hours per head block)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` consistent with previous runs\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` stable (no growth)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` stays < 50 (well-managed)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` stable or declining with retention\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Stuck compaction symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` == 1 for > 30 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` increasing unbounded\n- No increase in `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` for hours\n- Log shows same block being attempted repeatedly\n\n**Healthy vs. Problematic:**\n\n| Symptom | Healthy | Problematic |\n|---------|---------|------------|\n| Block count growth | Slow, consistent decline | Rapid, unbounded growth |\n| Compaction duration | Stable (±20%) | Increasing or wildly variable |\n| Failures counter | No growth | Growing at intervals |\n| WAL size | Stable or small | Growing unbounded |\n| CPU/Memory during compaction | Moderate spike, brief | Sustained high usage |\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` + WAL size ≈ available disk\n- Compaction errors: \"no space left on device\" or \"disk quota exceeded\"\n- New blocks fail to create in temporary directory\n- Prometheus error logs show: `open chunk writer: mkdir: no space left on device`\n- Prometheus becomes read-only or slow\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Retention duration too long**: `--storage.tsdb.retention.time` set too high\n- **Max bytes limit too high**: `--storage.tsdb.max-bytes` configured above available capacity\n- **Compaction not keeping pace**: Too much incoming data, compaction can't clean up fast enough\n- **Tombstones not being cleaned**: Deleted series not freed up by recompaction\n- **Temporary block accumulation**: Compaction failures leaving `.tmp-for-creation` directories\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check available disk space:**\n   ```bash\n   df -h <prometheus-data-dir>\n   du -sh <prometheus-data-dir>/wal\n   du -sh <prometheus-data-dir>/*.db  # Find largest blocks\n   ```\n\n2. **Identify block ages and sizes:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -lh <prometheus-data-dir> | grep -E '^d' | grep -oE '[0-9A-F]{26}'\n   ```\n\n3. **Check retention policies in config:**\n   ```bash\n   grep -E 'storage.tsdb.retention|max-bytes' prometheus.yml\n   ```\n\n4. **Inspect compaction metrics:**\n   ```\n   prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds (p95 > threshold)\n   ```\n\n5. **Check for stale `.tmp-for-deletion` or `.tmp-for-creation` directories:**\n   ```bash\n   find <prometheus-data-dir> -name \"*.tmp*\" -type d\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Option A: Immediate Relief (if retention can be reduced)**\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus gracefully:**\n   ```bash\n   kill -TERM <pid>  # Wait for graceful shutdown\n   ```\n\n2. **Delete old blocks manually (if safe):**\n   ```bash\n   # List blocks with times:\n   promtool tsdb list <prometheus-data-dir>\n\n   # Delete blocks older than cutoff (CAREFUL!):\n   # Blocks are ULID format (timestamp encoded in first part)\n   rm -rf <prometheus-data-dir>/01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV  # Example block\n   ```\n\n3. **Clean up temporary directories:**\n   ```bash\n   find <prometheus-data-dir> -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -o -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" | xargs rm -rf\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n**Option B: Reduce incoming data rate**\n\n1. **Identify top metrics consuming space:**\n   ```\n   topk(20, count by(__name__) ({job=\"<job>\"}))\n   ```\n\n2. **Drop metrics in scrape config:**\n   ```yaml\n   scrape_configs:\n     - job_name: 'problematic'\n       metric_relabel_configs:\n         - source_labels: [__name__]\n           regex: 'high_cardinality_metric_.*'\n           action: drop\n   ```\n\n3. **Reduce scrape intervals for non-critical metrics**\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus to apply changes**\n\n**Option C: Extend capacity (if not at limit)**\n\n1. **Check current retention settings:**\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/status | jq '.data.retention'\n   ```\n\n2. **If configured correctly, add more disk space**\n3. **Resume normal operations**\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` unchanged for hours\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` == 1 persistently\n- New blocks not created from WAL (head block not flushed)\n- Prometheus logs show no new compaction entries\n- High CPU or memory usage in compaction goroutine\n- Queries increasingly slow due to WAL size\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Context cancellation**: Compaction context canceled due to shutdown or timeout\n- **Index corruption**: Block index unreadable, preventing merge\n- **Memory pressure**: OOM killer targeting compaction process\n- **I/O bottleneck**: Storage subsystem overloaded (network storage, contention)\n- **Deadlock on locks**: Compaction mutex held by reload/retention operations\n- **Failed block marked unfixable**: Block with `Compaction.Failed = true` blocking plan\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check if compaction is running:**\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   # Look for high CPU/memory usage\n   ```\n\n2. **Check logs for errors:**\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compact\" prometheus.log | tail -50\n   grep -i \"failed\\|error\" prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify no zombie compactions:**\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep tsdb | grep -v grep\n   # Check for stuck processes\n   ```\n\n4. **Inspect block metadata for failures:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <prometheus-data-dir> | grep -i \"failed\\|compaction\"\n   ```\n\n5. **Check the compaction plan:**\n   ```\n   # Enable debug logging temporarily in Prometheus\n   # Restart with --log.level=debug\n   grep \"plan compaction\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor system resources:**\n   ```bash\n   top -p <prometheus-pid>\n   iostat -x 1 10  # Check I/O wait\n   free -h  # Check memory pressure\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n1. **If blocks marked as failed, unmark them:**\n\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n\n   # Read block meta\n   cat <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/meta.json\n\n   # Edit meta.json and set \"failed\": false\n   # OR use promtool (if available in your version):\n   promtool tsdb dump-meta <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/meta.json\n   ```\n\n2. **If index corruption suspected, delete and rebuild:**\n\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n\n   # Identify corrupt block\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <prometheus-data-dir>\n\n   # Delete corrupt block (if safe):\n   rm -rf <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>\n\n   # Restart Prometheus - it will re-compact head to replace missing block\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n3. **If stuck due to I/O, restart with priority change:**\n\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n   wait\n\n   # Restart with increased I/O priority (if supported):\n   nice -n -10 ionice -c2 -n0 prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n4. **If lock contention, increase retention check interval:**\n\n   Modify configuration to reduce concurrent operations:\n   ```yaml\n   global:\n     evaluation_interval: 5m  # Increase if very frequent\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor compaction resume:**\n   ```\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n   ```\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increasing\n- Errors like: \"corrupted block <ULID>: invalid chunk data\"\n- \"index out of bounds\" or \"checksum mismatch\" in logs\n- Specific block consistently fails to load\n- Query errors on certain time ranges\n- Prometheus won't start if corruption in critical block\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Hardware failure**: Bit flip, bad sector, or disk corruption\n- **Unclean shutdown**: Process killed during compaction or write\n- **Filesystem corruption**: Ext4, XFS, or storage layer corruption\n- **Concurrent writes**: Multiple Prometheus instances writing to same directory\n- **Out-of-disk-space write**: Block write failed mid-operation, file truncated\n- **Index version mismatch**: Older Prometheus version reading newer index format\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Identify corrupt blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <prometheus-data-dir>\n   # Look for blocks marked as \"corrupted\" or with read errors\n   ```\n\n2. **Check specific block validity:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump-blocks <prometheus-data-dir> <BLOCK-ULID>\n   # If it fails, block is corrupt\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify filesystem health:**\n   ```bash\n   sudo fsck -n <device>  # Non-destructive check\n   sudo badblocks -v <device>  # Find bad sectors\n   ```\n\n4. **Check hardware logs:**\n   ```bash\n   dmesg | grep -i \"error\\|corruption\\|io\"\n   journalctl -u prometheus -n 100  # Prometheus unit logs\n   ```\n\n5. **Inspect block directory manually:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -la <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/\n   file <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/{chunks,index,meta.json}\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Option A: Delete corrupt block (if it has backup/replacement)**\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify the block is safely deletable:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check if a newer block covers the time range\n   promtool tsdb list <prometheus-data-dir>\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete the corrupt block:**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf <prometheus-data-dir>/<CORRUPT-BLOCK-ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor recovery:**\n   ```bash\n   # Verify block is no longer in list\n   promtool tsdb list <prometheus-data-dir>\n\n   # Check metrics reload success\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total\n   ```\n\n**Option B: Attempt repair with promtool (if available)**\n\n```bash\n# Some versions of Prometheus include repair utilities\npromtool tsdb bench <prometheus-data-dir>  # Test if readable\n\n# Or manually edit meta.json if only metadata is corrupted\nvi <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/meta.json\n# Fix obvious issues (e.g., incorrect timestamps)\n```\n\n**Option C: Rebuild from WAL (if recent enough)**\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n2. **Back up corrupted blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   mkdir backup\n   mv <prometheus-data-dir>/0* backup/  # Move all blocks\n   ```\n\n3. **Start Prometheus with empty blocks directory:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   # It will rebuild from WAL\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor WAL replay:**\n   ```\n   grep \"replayed\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n#### Symptoms\n- Process killed with \"Killed\" or \"Segmentation fault\"\n- System logs show: \"Out of memory: Kill process\"\n- `dmesg` shows OOM killer invocation\n- Compaction fails midway without clean error\n- Memory usage spikes during `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block`\n- No error in Prometheus logs (process killed externally)\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Large block compaction**: Merging many or very large blocks simultaneously\n- **High cardinality data**: Too many unique metric/label combinations\n- **Insufficient memory**: System or container limit too low for data scale\n- **Memory leak in compaction**: Chunk pool not returning memory\n- **Concurrent operations**: Reload/retention cleanup + compaction both running\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check system memory during compaction:**\n   ```bash\n   # In separate terminal, watch while compaction runs\n   watch -n 1 'free -h && echo \"---\" && ps aux | grep prometheus'\n   ```\n\n2. **Check container/cgroup limits:**\n   ```bash\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory.limit_in_bytes  # If using cgroups\n   docker stats <container>  # If in container\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor memory at metric level:**\n   ```\n   process_resident_memory_bytes  # Watch during compaction\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block\n   ```\n\n4. **Check for memory pressure in logs:**\n   ```bash\n   dmesg | tail -20\n   journalctl --priority=warning\n   ```\n\n5. **Identify largest blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   du -h <prometheus-data-dir>/ | sort -h | tail -10\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n1. **Immediate: Increase system memory**\n   - Add more RAM to the system\n   - Or reduce container/Kubernetes memory limit restraint\n\n2. **Reduce block size (long-term solution):**\n\n   Stop Prometheus and adjust configuration:\n   ```yaml\n   global:\n     external_labels:\n       # Option A: Reduce maximum block duration\n       #tsdb.max-block-duration: 24h  # Down from default 36h\n   ```\n\n   Or in command line:\n   ```bash\n   prometheus --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=24h\n   ```\n\n3. **Reduce cardinality:**\n\n   ```yaml\n   scrape_configs:\n     - job_name: 'high_cardinality'\n       metric_relabel_configs:\n         - source_labels: [__name__]\n           regex: 'bad_metric_.*'\n           action: drop\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus with new settings:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor compaction:**\n   - Should take longer but succeed with reduced memory\n   - Check `process_resident_memory_bytes` stays below limit\n\n6. **If recurring, consider splitting Prometheus instances:**\n   - Use separate instances for different jobs\n   - Use federation instead of single monolithic instance\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Pre-Recovery Checklist\n\nBefore attempting recovery:\n\n1. **Gather diagnostic information:**\n   ```bash\n   date > recovery.log\n   df -h >> recovery.log\n   ps aux | grep prometheus >> recovery.log\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/status >> recovery.log\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <data-dir> >> recovery.log 2>&1\n   ```\n\n2. **Back up data directory:**\n   ```bash\n   cp -r <prometheus-data-dir> <prometheus-data-dir>.backup.$(date +%s)\n   ```\n\n3. **Document current state:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -la <prometheus-data-dir> > before_recovery.txt\n   ```\n\n### When to Restart Prometheus vs. Manual Intervention\n\n| Situation | Action | Rationale |\n|-----------|--------|-----------|\n| Compaction stuck but no errors | Restart | Clean restart often clears transient lock issues |\n| Disk full | Reduce retention first | Manual deletion required before restart |\n| Corrupted block, recent backup exists | Delete block | Prevents read errors on startup |\n| Failed block with `Compaction.Failed=true` | Edit meta.json | Allows planner to retry or skip block |\n| Memory exhaustion | Increase memory + restart | Restart with new limits |\n| I/O overload | Reduce concurrency | Adjust config before restart |\n\n### Step-by-Step Generic Recovery\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   # Graceful stop (preferred)\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n   sleep 30\n\n   # If not stopped, force\n   kill -9 <pid>\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify all processes stopped:**\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   ```\n\n3. **Backup current state:**\n   ```bash\n   tar czf prometheus-data-$(date +%s).tar.gz <data-dir>\n   ```\n\n4. **Apply failure-specific recovery** (see sections above)\n\n5. **Start Prometheus with clean state:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus \\\n     --storage.tsdb.path=<data-dir> \\\n     --log.level=info \\\n     <other flags>\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor startup and recovery:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch logs\n   tail -f prometheus.log\n\n   # Or in separate terminal\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\n   ```\n\n7. **Verify metrics health:**\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n   ```\n\n### Using `promtool` for Inspection and Repair\n\n#### Inspect All Blocks\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb inspect-blocks <data-dir>\n\n# Output example:\n# Block ID: 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\n#   Compaction level: 1\n#   Created: <timestamp>\n#   Min time: 1609459200000\n#   Max time: 1609545600000\n#   Series: 10000\n#   Samples: 5000000\n```\n\n#### List Blocks\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb list <data-dir>\n\n# Output example:\n# ULID                         MinTime                 MaxTime                 Duration  NumSeries  NumSamples  NumTombstones  Compaction\n# 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV   2021-01-01T00:00:00Z   2021-01-02T00:00:00Z   24h       10000      5000000     0              Level: 1\n```\n\n#### Dump Block Metadata\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb dump-meta <data-dir>/<block-id>/meta.json\n\n# Shows full metadata including:\n# - Compaction level\n# - Parents (source blocks)\n# - Sources (original blocks)\n# - Stats (samples, series, tombstones)\n```\n\n#### Bench/Validate Block\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb bench read <data-dir> --duration=1h\n\n# Validates all blocks can be read successfully\n```\n\n#### WAL Repair (if available)\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb list-wbl <data-dir>/wal\n# Lists write-ahead log blocks\n\n# Or for WAL directory:\npromtool tsdb dump-wal <data-dir>/wal | head -100\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Runbook Quick Reference\n\n### Emergency Contacts / Escalation\n\n- **Storage team**: For disk/I/O issues\n- **Infrastructure team**: For memory/CPU constraints\n- **Database team**: For corruption/data integrity issues\n\n### Common Commands\n\n```bash\n# Gracefully stop\nkill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n\n# Check compaction status\ncurl http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n\n# List blocks\npromtool tsdb list <data-dir>\n\n# Inspect block\npromtool tsdb inspect-blocks <data-dir>\n\n# Backup before recovery\ntar czf tsdb-backup.tar.gz <data-dir>\n\n# Monitor logs\ntail -f prometheus.log | grep -i compact\n\n# Check disk usage\ndu -sh <data-dir>\ndf -h <data-dir>\n```\n\n### Decision Tree\n\n```\nCompaction Issue Detected\n│\n├─> No errors in logs\n│   └─> Might be normal, check:\n│       └─> prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total increasing?\n│           ├─> YES: Normal, relax\n│           └─> NO: Stuck → Restart Prometheus\n│\n├─> \"no space left on device\"\n│   └─> Disk space recovery (Section 3.1)\n│\n├─> \"corrupted block\"\n│   └─> Block corruption recovery (Section 3.3)\n│\n├─> Stuck for hours + high memory\n│   └─> OOM recovery (Section 3.4)\n│\n├─> Compaction timeout or context canceled\n│   └─> Stuck compaction recovery (Section 3.2)\n│\n└─> Uncertain\n    └─> Run diagnostics, check all metrics\n        └─> Review monitoring indicators (Section 2)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Configuration Reference\n\n### Relevant Prometheus Flags\n\n```bash\n# Block compaction\n--storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=2h      # Flush head block interval\n--storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=36h     # Max compacted block size\n\n# Retention policies\n--storage.tsdb.retention.time=15d         # Keep data for 15 days\n--storage.tsdb.retention.size=50GB        # Or keep up to 50GB\n\n# Compaction behavior\n--storage.tsdb.wal-compression=snappy     # WAL compression (reduces size)\n--storage.tsdb.samples-per-chunk=1024     # Samples per chunk (affects compaction mem)\n\n# Resource management\n--storage.tsdb.max-wal-duration=1h        # WAL flush interval\n--query.max-samples=1000000               # Prevents large queries during compaction\n```\n\n### Typical Production Setup\n\n```bash\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.path=/var/lib/prometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.size=500GB \\\n  --storage.tsdb.wal-compression=snappy \\\n  --storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=2h \\\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=12h \\\n  --web.listen-address=:9090 \\\n  --config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n```\n\n---\n\n**Last Updated**: 2024\n**Prometheus Version**: v2.52.0\n**Runbook Version**: 1.0\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":2298,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1298,"cache_read_input_tokens":52674,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1298},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c95aba4c-9f56-462a-a067-b43e0d2be34e","uuid":"38e94bae-a4cc-4b0b-84d6-6e16c40da1fc"}

Overview\n\n### What Compaction Does\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction is a crucial maintenance process that merges overlapping time blocks, removes tombstoned series, and maintains query performance over time. The compaction process:\n\n- **Merges overlapping blocks**: Combines blocks with overlapping time ranges into a single, deduplicated block\n- **Removes deleted series**: Reclaims disk space by eliminating tombstoned (deleted) series data\n- **Reorganizes data**: Creates larger, better-structured blocks for improved query efficiency\n- **Manages WAL**: Converts in-memory Write-Ahead Log (WAL) data into persisted blocks\n\n### Why Compaction Is Needed\n\nWithout compaction, Prometheus would:\n- Accumulate many small blocks, slowing down queries\n- Retain deleted data indefinitely, wasting disk space\n- Have fragmented data with overlapping time ranges causing inefficient query execution\n- Build up an excessively large WAL\n\n### Compaction Levels and Block Structure\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction** strategy with exponential block ranges:\n\n- **Level 0 blocks**: Raw blocks created directly from WAL data (2 hours by default, `MinBlockDuration`)\n- **Level 1+ blocks**: Result of compacting multiple Level 0 blocks\n- **Block ranges**: By default: 2h, 6h, 18h, 54h, 162h, etc. (exponential with step size 3)\n\nEach block is identified by:\n- **ULID**: Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier with timestamp\n- **MinTime/MaxTime**: Time range of data in milliseconds\n- **Compaction.Level**: Current compaction level\n- **Compaction.Parents**: References to source blocks\n\n### When Compaction Is Triggered\n\n#### Time-Based (Automatic)\n\nCompaction triggers when the head block reaches `MinBlockDuration` (2 hours):\n\n1. **Head block compaction**: When `head.compactable()` returns true\n   - Head contains data older than MinBlockDuration/2\n   - Triggered in the main compaction goroutine loop\n   - Result: New persistent block created, WAL truncated\n\n2. **Block merging**: Triggered by the compaction plan\n   - Blocks are selected for merging based on size and level\n   - Selection follows `LeveledCompactor.selectDirs()` logic\n   - Algorithm ensures blocks are merged level-by-level\n\n#### Size-Based (Opportunistic)\n\nThe compaction planner also triggers compaction for:\n- **Tombstone cleanup**: Blocks with >5% deleted series (tombstones) are recompacted\n- **Overlapping blocks**: Vertical compaction for blocks with overlapping time ranges\n- **Failed blocks**: Blocks marked with `Compaction.Failed` are skipped in subsequent plans\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\nMonitor these metrics to track compaction health:\n\n#### Compaction Execution\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | N/A (baseline) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total triggered compactions | Rapid increase indicates issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions | > 0 (indicates failures) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Compaction execution time | P95 > 5min suggests slowdown |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to disabled auto-compact | Increases if manual intervention |\n\n#### Block Management\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded persistent blocks | > 100 (too many blocks) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total block storage size in bytes | Approaches max or disk limit |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max block retention bytes | Should match config |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases with out-of-order data |\n\n#### Compaction Progress\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Currently writing block (1 = in progress) | Should return to 0 |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact for tombstone removal | P95 > 30s suggests large blocks |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Behavior\n\n**Healthy indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increases regularly (every 2-5 hours per head block)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` consistent with previous runs\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` stable (no growth)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` stays < 50 (well-managed)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` stable or declining with retention\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Stuck compaction symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` == 1 for > 30 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` increasing unbounded\n- No increase in `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` for hours\n- Log shows same block being attempted repeatedly\n\n**Healthy vs. Problematic:**\n\n| Symptom | Healthy | Problematic |\n|---------|---------|------------|\n| Block count growth | Slow, consistent decline | Rapid, unbounded growth |\n| Compaction duration | Stable (±20%) | Increasing or wildly variable |\n| Failures counter | No growth | Growing at intervals |\n| WAL size | Stable or small | Growing unbounded |\n| CPU/Memory during compaction | Moderate spike, brief | Sustained high usage |\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` + WAL size ≈ available disk\n- Compaction errors: \"no space left on device\" or \"disk quota exceeded\"\n- New blocks fail to create in temporary directory\n- Prometheus error logs show: `open chunk writer: mkdir: no space left on device`\n- Prometheus becomes read-only or slow\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Retention duration too long**: `--storage.tsdb.retention.time` set too high\n- **Max bytes limit too high**: `--storage.tsdb.max-bytes` configured above available capacity\n- **Compaction not keeping pace**: Too much incoming data, compaction can't clean up fast enough\n- **Tombstones not being cleaned**: Deleted series not freed up by recompaction\n- **Temporary block accumulation**: Compaction failures leaving `.tmp-for-creation` directories\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check available disk space:**\n   ```bash\n   df -h <prometheus-data-dir>\n   du -sh <prometheus-data-dir>/wal\n   du -sh <prometheus-data-dir>/*.db  # Find largest blocks\n   ```\n\n2. **Identify block ages and sizes:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -lh <prometheus-data-dir> | grep -E '^d' | grep -oE '[0-9A-F]{26}'\n   ```\n\n3. **Check retention policies in config:**\n   ```bash\n   grep -E 'storage.tsdb.retention|max-bytes' prometheus.yml\n   ```\n\n4. **Inspect compaction metrics:**\n   ```\n   prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds (p95 > threshold)\n   ```\n\n5. **Check for stale `.tmp-for-deletion` or `.tmp-for-creation` directories:**\n   ```bash\n   find <prometheus-data-dir> -name \"*.tmp*\" -type d\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Option A: Immediate Relief (if retention can be reduced)**\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus gracefully:**\n   ```bash\n   kill -TERM <pid>  # Wait for graceful shutdown\n   ```\n\n2. **Delete old blocks manually (if safe):**\n   ```bash\n   # List blocks with times:\n   promtool tsdb list <prometheus-data-dir>\n\n   # Delete blocks older than cutoff (CAREFUL!):\n   # Blocks are ULID format (timestamp encoded in first part)\n   rm -rf <prometheus-data-dir>/01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV  # Example block\n   ```\n\n3. **Clean up temporary directories:**\n   ```bash\n   find <prometheus-data-dir> -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -o -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" | xargs rm -rf\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n**Option B: Reduce incoming data rate**\n\n1. **Identify top metrics consuming space:**\n   ```\n   topk(20, count by(__name__) ({job=\"<job>\"}))\n   ```\n\n2. **Drop metrics in scrape config:**\n   ```yaml\n   scrape_configs:\n     - job_name: 'problematic'\n       metric_relabel_configs:\n         - source_labels: [__name__]\n           regex: 'high_cardinality_metric_.*'\n           action: drop\n   ```\n\n3. **Reduce scrape intervals for non-critical metrics**\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus to apply changes**\n\n**Option C: Extend capacity (if not at limit)**\n\n1. **Check current retention settings:**\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/status | jq '.data.retention'\n   ```\n\n2. **If configured correctly, add more disk space**\n3. **Resume normal operations**\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` unchanged for hours\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` == 1 persistently\n- New blocks not created from WAL (head block not flushed)\n- Prometheus logs show no new compaction entries\n- High CPU or memory usage in compaction goroutine\n- Queries increasingly slow due to WAL size\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Context cancellation**: Compaction context canceled due to shutdown or timeout\n- **Index corruption**: Block index unreadable, preventing merge\n- **Memory pressure**: OOM killer targeting compaction process\n- **I/O bottleneck**: Storage subsystem overloaded (network storage, contention)\n- **Deadlock on locks**: Compaction mutex held by reload/retention operations\n- **Failed block marked unfixable**: Block with `Compaction.Failed = true` blocking plan\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check if compaction is running:**\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   # Look for high CPU/memory usage\n   ```\n\n2. **Check logs for errors:**\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compact\" prometheus.log | tail -50\n   grep -i \"failed\\|error\" prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify no zombie compactions:**\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep tsdb | grep -v grep\n   # Check for stuck processes\n   ```\n\n4. **Inspect block metadata for failures:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <prometheus-data-dir> | grep -i \"failed\\|compaction\"\n   ```\n\n5. **Check the compaction plan:**\n   ```\n   # Enable debug logging temporarily in Prometheus\n   # Restart with --log.level=debug\n   grep \"plan compaction\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor system resources:**\n   ```bash\n   top -p <prometheus-pid>\n   iostat -x 1 10  # Check I/O wait\n   free -h  # Check memory pressure\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n1. **If blocks marked as failed, unmark them:**\n\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n\n   # Read block meta\n   cat <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/meta.json\n\n   # Edit meta.json and set \"failed\": false\n   # OR use promtool (if available in your version):\n   promtool tsdb dump-meta <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/meta.json\n   ```\n\n2. **If index corruption suspected, delete and rebuild:**\n\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n\n   # Identify corrupt block\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <prometheus-data-dir>\n\n   # Delete corrupt block (if safe):\n   rm -rf <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>\n\n   # Restart Prometheus - it will re-compact head to replace missing block\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n3. **If stuck due to I/O, restart with priority change:**\n\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n   wait\n\n   # Restart with increased I/O priority (if supported):\n   nice -n -10 ionice -c2 -n0 prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n4. **If lock contention, increase retention check interval:**\n\n   Modify configuration to reduce concurrent operations:\n   ```yaml\n   global:\n     evaluation_interval: 5m  # Increase if very frequent\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor compaction resume:**\n   ```\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n   ```\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increasing\n- Errors like: \"corrupted block <ULID>: invalid chunk data\"\n- \"index out of bounds\" or \"checksum mismatch\" in logs\n- Specific block consistently fails to load\n- Query errors on certain time ranges\n- Prometheus won't start if corruption in critical block\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Hardware failure**: Bit flip, bad sector, or disk corruption\n- **Unclean shutdown**: Process killed during compaction or write\n- **Filesystem corruption**: Ext4, XFS, or storage layer corruption\n- **Concurrent writes**: Multiple Prometheus instances writing to same directory\n- **Out-of-disk-space write**: Block write failed mid-operation, file truncated\n- **Index version mismatch**: Older Prometheus version reading newer index format\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Identify corrupt blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <prometheus-data-dir>\n   # Look for blocks marked as \"corrupted\" or with read errors\n   ```\n\n2. **Check specific block validity:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump-blocks <prometheus-data-dir> <BLOCK-ULID>\n   # If it fails, block is corrupt\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify filesystem health:**\n   ```bash\n   sudo fsck -n <device>  # Non-destructive check\n   sudo badblocks -v <device>  # Find bad sectors\n   ```\n\n4. **Check hardware logs:**\n   ```bash\n   dmesg | grep -i \"error\\|corruption\\|io\"\n   journalctl -u prometheus -n 100  # Prometheus unit logs\n   ```\n\n5. **Inspect block directory manually:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -la <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/\n   file <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/{chunks,index,meta.json}\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Option A: Delete corrupt block (if it has backup/replacement)**\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify the block is safely deletable:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check if a newer block covers the time range\n   promtool tsdb list <prometheus-data-dir>\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete the corrupt block:**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf <prometheus-data-dir>/<CORRUPT-BLOCK-ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor recovery:**\n   ```bash\n   # Verify block is no longer in list\n   promtool tsdb list <prometheus-data-dir>\n\n   # Check metrics reload success\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total\n   ```\n\n**Option B: Attempt repair with promtool (if available)**\n\n```bash\n# Some versions of Prometheus include repair utilities\npromtool tsdb bench <prometheus-data-dir>  # Test if readable\n\n# Or manually edit meta.json if only metadata is corrupted\nvi <prometheus-data-dir>/<BLOCK-ULID>/meta.json\n# Fix obvious issues (e.g., incorrect timestamps)\n```\n\n**Option C: Rebuild from WAL (if recent enough)**\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n2. **Back up corrupted blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   mkdir backup\n   mv <prometheus-data-dir>/0* backup/  # Move all blocks\n   ```\n\n3. **Start Prometheus with empty blocks directory:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   # It will rebuild from WAL\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor WAL replay:**\n   ```\n   grep \"replayed\" prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n#### Symptoms\n- Process killed with \"Killed\" or \"Segmentation fault\"\n- System logs show: \"Out of memory: Kill process\"\n- `dmesg` shows OOM killer invocation\n- Compaction fails midway without clean error\n- Memory usage spikes during `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block`\n- No error in Prometheus logs (process killed externally)\n\n#### Likely Causes\n- **Large block compaction**: Merging many or very large blocks simultaneously\n- **High cardinality data**: Too many unique metric/label combinations\n- **Insufficient memory**: System or container limit too low for data scale\n- **Memory leak in compaction**: Chunk pool not returning memory\n- **Concurrent operations**: Reload/retention cleanup + compaction both running\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check system memory during compaction:**\n   ```bash\n   # In separate terminal, watch while compaction runs\n   watch -n 1 'free -h && echo \"---\" && ps aux | grep prometheus'\n   ```\n\n2. **Check container/cgroup limits:**\n   ```bash\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory.limit_in_bytes  # If using cgroups\n   docker stats <container>  # If in container\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor memory at metric level:**\n   ```\n   process_resident_memory_bytes  # Watch during compaction\n   prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block\n   ```\n\n4. **Check for memory pressure in logs:**\n   ```bash\n   dmesg | tail -20\n   journalctl --priority=warning\n   ```\n\n5. **Identify largest blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   du -h <prometheus-data-dir>/ | sort -h | tail -10\n   ```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n1. **Immediate: Increase system memory**\n   - Add more RAM to the system\n   - Or reduce container/Kubernetes memory limit restraint\n\n2. **Reduce block size (long-term solution):**\n\n   Stop Prometheus and adjust configuration:\n   ```yaml\n   global:\n     external_labels:\n       # Option A: Reduce maximum block duration\n       #tsdb.max-block-duration: 24h  # Down from default 36h\n   ```\n\n   Or in command line:\n   ```bash\n   prometheus --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=24h\n   ```\n\n3. **Reduce cardinality:**\n\n   ```yaml\n   scrape_configs:\n     - job_name: 'high_cardinality'\n       metric_relabel_configs:\n         - source_labels: [__name__]\n           regex: 'bad_metric_.*'\n           action: drop\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus with new settings:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus <flags>\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor compaction:**\n   - Should take longer but succeed with reduced memory\n   - Check `process_resident_memory_bytes` stays below limit\n\n6. **If recurring, consider splitting Prometheus instances:**\n   - Use separate instances for different jobs\n   - Use federation instead of single monolithic instance\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Pre-Recovery Checklist\n\nBefore attempting recovery:\n\n1. **Gather diagnostic information:**\n   ```bash\n   date > recovery.log\n   df -h >> recovery.log\n   ps aux | grep prometheus >> recovery.log\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/status >> recovery.log\n   promtool tsdb inspect-blocks <data-dir> >> recovery.log 2>&1\n   ```\n\n2. **Back up data directory:**\n   ```bash\n   cp -r <prometheus-data-dir> <prometheus-data-dir>.backup.$(date +%s)\n   ```\n\n3. **Document current state:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -la <prometheus-data-dir> > before_recovery.txt\n   ```\n\n### When to Restart Prometheus vs. Manual Intervention\n\n| Situation | Action | Rationale |\n|-----------|--------|-----------|\n| Compaction stuck but no errors | Restart | Clean restart often clears transient lock issues |\n| Disk full | Reduce retention first | Manual deletion required before restart |\n| Corrupted block, recent backup exists | Delete block | Prevents read errors on startup |\n| Failed block with `Compaction.Failed=true` | Edit meta.json | Allows planner to retry or skip block |\n| Memory exhaustion | Increase memory + restart | Restart with new limits |\n| I/O overload | Reduce concurrency | Adjust config before restart |\n\n### Step-by-Step Generic Recovery\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus:**\n   ```bash\n   # Graceful stop (preferred)\n   kill -TERM <pid>\n   sleep 30\n\n   # If not stopped, force\n   kill -9 <pid>\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify all processes stopped:**\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   ```\n\n3. **Backup current state:**\n   ```bash\n   tar czf prometheus-data-$(date +%s).tar.gz <data-dir>\n   ```\n\n4. **Apply failure-specific recovery** (see sections above)\n\n5. **Start Prometheus with clean state:**\n   ```bash\n   prometheus \\\n     --storage.tsdb.path=<data-dir> \\\n     --log.level=info \\\n     <other flags>\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor startup and recovery:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch logs\n   tail -f prometheus.log\n\n   # Or in separate terminal\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\n   ```\n\n7. **Verify metrics health:**\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n   ```\n\n### Using `promtool` for Inspection and Repair\n\n#### Inspect All Blocks\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb inspect-blocks <data-dir>\n\n# Output example:\n# Block ID: 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\n#   Compaction level: 1\n#   Created: <timestamp>\n#   Min time: 1609459200000\n#   Max time: 1609545600000\n#   Series: 10000\n#   Samples: 5000000\n```\n\n#### List Blocks\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb list <data-dir>\n\n# Output example:\n# ULID                         MinTime                 MaxTime                 Duration  NumSeries  NumSamples  NumTombstones  Compaction\n# 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV   2021-01-01T00:00:00Z   2021-01-02T00:00:00Z   24h       10000      5000000     0              Level: 1\n```\n\n#### Dump Block Metadata\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb dump-meta <data-dir>/<block-id>/meta.json\n\n# Shows full metadata including:\n# - Compaction level\n# - Parents (source blocks)\n# - Sources (original blocks)\n# - Stats (samples, series, tombstones)\n```\n\n#### Bench/Validate Block\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb bench read <data-dir> --duration=1h\n\n# Validates all blocks can be read successfully\n```\n\n#### WAL Repair (if available)\n\n```bash\npromtool tsdb list-wbl <data-dir>/wal\n# Lists write-ahead log blocks\n\n# Or for WAL directory:\npromtool tsdb dump-wal <data-dir>/wal | head -100\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code Reference\n\n### Key Functions by Failure Mode\n\n#### Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n| Component | File | Function | Relevance |\n|-----------|------|----------|-----------|\n| Block lifecycle | `tsdb/block.go` | `setCompactionFailed()` line 456 | Marks failed blocks to avoid retry |\n| Compaction write | `tsdb/compact.go` | `write()` line 607 | Creates `.tmp-for-creation`, handles disk errors at line 626-627 |\n| Cleanup | `tsdb/db.go` | `reloadBlocks()` line 1426 | Marks blocks deletable (line 1445) |\n| Retention | `tsdb/db.go` | `deleteBlocks()` | Removes old/large blocks based on retention policy |\n\n**Relevant error handling:**\n- `tsdb/compact.go:622-627` - `os.RemoveAll(tmp)` and `os.MkdirAll(tmp)` - disk space check\n- `tsdb/compact.go:634` - `chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize()` - fails if no space\n- `tsdb/db.go:1382-1384` - Compact error handling in `compactBlocks()`\n\n#### Compaction Stuck/Not Progressing\n\n| Component | File | Function | Relevance |\n|-----------|------|----------|-----------|\n| Trigger condition | `tsdb/head.go` | `compactable()` | Determines if head should be flushed |\n| Compaction loop | `tsdb/db.go` | `runCompaction()` | Main compaction goroutine (line ~1000) |\n| Plan selection | `tsdb/compact.go` | `Plan()` line 222, `plan()` line 242 | Selects blocks to compact |\n| Block selection | `tsdb/compact.go` | `selectDirs()` line 291 | Selects blocks, skips failed ones (line 308) |\n| Mutex lock | `tsdb/db.go` | `cmtx sync.Mutex` line 224 | Protects compaction operations |\n| Context check | `tsdb/compact.go` | `write()` line 659-662 | Respects context cancellation |\n\n**Relevant entry points:**\n- `tsdb/db.go:1008` - `case <-db.compactc:` - receives compaction signal\n- `tsdb/db.go:1120-1123` - `head.compactable()` check triggers compaction\n- `tsdb/compact.go:528-534` - Failed block marking on error\n\n#### Block Corruption\n\n| Component | File | Function | Relevance |\n|-----------|------|----------|-----------|\n| Block loading | `tsdb/block.go` | `OpenBlock()` | Opens and validates block structure |\n| Index reading | `tsdb/compact.go` | PopulateBlock() line 769-791 | Reads index, returns errors if corrupt |\n| Reload | `tsdb/db.go` | `reloadBlocks()` line 1426 | Detects corrupted blocks (line 1463-1478) |\n| Failure marking | `tsdb/compact.go` | `CompactWithBlockPopulator()` line 528-534 | Marks block failed on error |\n| Error types | `tsdb/block.go` | Block open errors | Returns wrapped errors with context |\n\n**Error detection:**\n- `tsdb/db.go:1440-1443` - `openBlocks()` detects and returns corrupted blocks map\n- `tsdb/db.go:1463-1478` - Handles corrupted blocks, prevents loading if corruption\n\n#### Out-of-Memory (OOM)\n\n| Component | File | Function | Relevance |\n|-----------|------|----------|-----------|\n| Chunk pool | `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go` | Chunk memory management | Reuses buffers to reduce allocations |\n| PopulateBlock | `tsdb/compact.go` | `PopulateBlock()` line 729 | Core memory consumer during merge |\n| Series merge | `storage/merge.go` | Vertical merge function | Merges overlapping series (memory-heavy) |\n| Context | `tsdb/compact.go` | `write()` line 659-662 | Respects context to stop early on cancel |\n| Metrics | `tsdb/compact.go` | `PopulatingBlocks` line 107 | Gauge shows when compacting (line 748, 746) |\n\n**Memory pressure points:**\n- `tsdb/compact.go:655` - `blockPopulator.PopulateBlock()` - main memory consumer\n- `tsdb/compact.go:748` - `metrics.PopulatingBlocks.Set(1)` - indicates active memory usage\n\n### Monitoring Metrics (Implementation)\n\nFound in `tsdb/compact.go:89-97` (CompactorMetrics) and `tsdb/db.go:244-259` (dbMetrics):\n\n```go\n// Compaction metrics\nprometheus_tsdb_compactions_total                    // line 104\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds          // line 116\nprometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total           // line 112\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block          // line 108\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes          // line 124\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples             // line 129\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds       // line 134\n\n// DB metrics\nprometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total          // line 294\nprometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total             // line 297\nprometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total            // line 305\nprometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded                        // line 265\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes                 // line 328\nprometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes                // line 332\nprometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds            // line 321\n```\n\n### Critical Structures\n\n**BlockMeta** (`tsdb/block.go`):\n- `ULID`: Block identifier\n- `MinTime, MaxTime`: Time range\n- `Compaction.Level`: Level in hierarchy\n- `Compaction.Failed`: Prevents retry\n- `Stats`: NumSamples, NumTombstones, NumSeries\n\n**LeveledCompactor** (`tsdb/compact.go:76-87`):\n- `ranges`: Block duration hierarchy\n- `enableOverlappingCompaction`: Vertical compaction flag\n- `metrics`: Observability\n- `ctx`: Context for cancellation\n\n**DB** (`tsdb/db.go:198-242`):\n- `compactc`: Signal channel for compaction trigger\n- `cmtx`: Mutex protecting compaction operations\n- `autoCompact`: Whether compaction is enabled\n- `head`: In-memory buffer with `compactable()` method\n\n---\n\n## 6. Runbook Quick Reference\n\n### Emergency Contacts / Escalation\n\n- **Storage team**: For disk/I/O issues\n- **Infrastructure team**: For memory/CPU constraints\n- **Database team**: For corruption/data integrity issues\n\n### Common Commands\n\n```bash\n# Gracefully stop\nkill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n\n# Check compaction status\ncurl http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n\n# List blocks\npromtool tsdb list <data-dir>\n\n# Inspect block\npromtool tsdb inspect-blocks <data-dir>\n\n# Backup before recovery\ntar czf tsdb-backup.tar.gz <data-dir>\n\n# Monitor logs\ntail -f prometheus.log | grep -i compact\n\n# Check disk usage\ndu -sh <data-dir>\ndf -h <data-dir>\n```\n\n### Decision Tree\n\n```\nCompaction Issue Detected\n│\n├─> No errors in logs\n│   └─> Might be normal, check:\n│       └─> prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total increasing?\n│           ├─> YES: Normal, relax\n│           └─> NO: Stuck → Restart Prometheus\n│\n├─> \"no space left on device\"\n│   └─> Disk space recovery (Section 3.1)\n│\n├─> \"corrupted block\"\n│   └─> Block corruption recovery (Section 3.3)\n│\n├─> Stuck for hours + high memory\n│   └─> OOM recovery (Section 3.4)\n│\n├─> Compaction timeout or context canceled\n│   └─> Stuck compaction recovery (Section 3.2)\n│\n└─> Uncertain\n    └─> Run diagnostics, check all metrics\n        └─> Review monitoring indicators (Section 2)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Configuration Reference\n\n### Relevant Prometheus Flags\n\n```bash\n# Block compaction\n--storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=2h      # Flush head block interval\n--storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=36h     # Max compacted block size\n\n# Retention policies\n--storage.tsdb.retention.time=15d         # Keep data for 15 days\n--storage.tsdb.retention.size=50GB        # Or keep up to 50GB\n\n# Compaction behavior\n--storage.tsdb.wal-compression=snappy     # WAL compression (reduces size)\n--storage.tsdb.samples-per-chunk=1024     # Samples per chunk (affects compaction mem)\n\n# Resource management\n--storage.tsdb.max-wal-duration=1h        # WAL flush interval\n--query.max-samples=1000000               # Prevents large queries during compaction\n```\n\n### Typical Production Setup\n\n```bash\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.path=/var/lib/prometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.size=500GB \\\n  --storage.tsdb.wal-compression=snappy \\\n  --storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=2h \\\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=12h \\\n  --web.listen-address=:9090 \\\n  --config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n```\n\n---\n\n**Last Updated**: 2024\n**Prometheus Version**: v2.52.0\n**Runbook Version**: 1.0\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
